              (89,'Actinium','Actinium','Ac'),
              <br/>
              (90,'Thorium','Thorium','Th'),
              <br/>
              (91,'Protactinium','Protactinium','Pa'),
              <br/>
              (92,'Uranium','Uranium','U'),
              <br/>
              (93,'Neptunium','Neptunium','Np'),
              <br/>
              (94,'Plutonium','Plutonium','Pu'),
              <br/>
              (95,'Americium','Americium','Am'),
              <br/>
              (96,'Curium','Curium','Cm'),
              <br/>
              (97,'Berkelium','Berkelium','Bk'),
              <br/>
              (98,'Californium','Californium','Cf'),
              <br/>
              (99,'Einsteinium','Einsteinium','Es'),
              <br/>
              (100,'Fermium','Fermium','Fm'),
              <br/>
              (101,'Mendelevium','Mendelevium','Md'),
              <br/>
              (102,'Nobelium','Nobelium','No'),
              <br/>
              (103,'Lawrencium','Lawrencium','Lr'),
              <br/>
              (104,'Rutherfordium','Rutherfordium','Rf'),
              <br/>
              (105,'Dubnium','Dubnium','Db'),
              <br/>
              (106,'Seaborgium','Seaborgium','Sg'),
              <br/>
              (107,'Bohrium','Bohrium','Bh'),
              <br/>
              (108,'Hassium','Hassium','Hs'),
              <br/>
              (109,'Meitnerium','Meitnerium','Mt')
              <br/>
              "
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***runthesqlquery***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              if(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysql_query
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $link
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ))
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Newrecordcreatedsuccessfully&lt;br/&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              else
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'UnabletoINSERTdata:&lt;br/&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;br/&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysql_error
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ();
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***ifweareunabletoselectthedatabaseshowanerror***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              else
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Unabletoselectdatabase'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***closetheconnection***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysql_close
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $link
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              else
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***ifwefailtoconnect***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Unabletoconnect'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              ?&gt;
              <br/>
             </span>
            </span>
           </code>
          </div>
          <p>
           The above code will populate the elements table with all one hundred and nine elements. This is far superior to one hundred and nine seperate INSERT statements and database connections. Be aware that of the Max Allowed Packet size as large SQL statements of several thousand INSERTs or BLOBs may breach this limit.
          </p>
          <h4>
           <a class="anchor" name="8.2">
            INSERT multiple records with mysqli
           </a>
          </h4>
          <p>
           The mysqli extenstion provides an object oriented approach to the same task. The mysqli extension contains a class method named multi_query() for exactly this purpose. This class method basically takes an SQL statement, or multiple SQL statements concatenated by a semicolon
           <span class="codechar">
            ;
           </span>
           character. Lets see it in action with a small subset of our periodic table of elements. We use a subset because I had to type that first lot out and it took me hours ...
          </p>
          <div class="codebox">
           <code>
            <span style="color: #000000">
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              &lt;?php
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlhostname***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $hostname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'localhost'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlusername***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $username
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'username'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlpassword***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $password
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'password'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqldatabasename***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'periodic_table'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***createanewmysqliobjectwithdefaultdatabase***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $mysqli
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =@new
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysqli
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $hostname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $username
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $password
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /*checkconnection*/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              if(!
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysqli_connect_errno
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ())
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***ifwearesuccessful***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'ConnectedSuccessfully&lt;br/&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***sqltoINSERTanewrecord***/
              <br/>
              /***notethesemicolonontheendofeachstatement***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "INSERTINTOelements(atomicnumber,latin,english,abbr)VALUES(1,'HYDROGENIUM','Hydrogen','H');"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .=
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "INSERTINTOelements(atomicnumber,latin,english,abbr)VALUES(2,'HELIUM','Helium','He');"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .=
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "INSERTINTOelements(atomicnumber,latin,english,abbr)VALUES(3,'LITHIUM','Lithium','Li')"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .=
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "INSERTINTOelements(atomicnumber,latin,english,abbr)VALUES(4,'BERYLLIUM','Beryllium','Be');"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .=
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "INSERTINTOelements(atomicnumber,latin,english,abbr)VALUES(5,'BORUM','Boron','B')"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***runthemultiplestatementsandcheckforerrors***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              if(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $mysqli
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              multi_query
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              )!==
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              FALSE
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              )
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Newrecordscreatedsuccessfully&lt;br/&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              else
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;br/&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $mysqli
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              error
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***closeconnection***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $mysqli
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              close
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ();
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              else
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***ifweareunabletoconnect***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Unabletoconnect'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              exit();
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              ?&gt;
              <br/>
             </span>
            </span>
           </code>
          </div>
          <p>
           The above, shortened INSERT will work for the whole table and it is left as an exercise for the reader to complete the table. The mysqli extension provides a second method for achieving the same result for multiple INSERT. We can also use prepared statements and bind parameters. The mysql extension can send a statement or query without any data to the mysql database. You can then associate or "bind" variables to the columns.
          </p>
          <div class="codebox">
           <code>
            <span style="color: #000000">
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              &lt;?php
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlhostname***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $hostname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'localhost'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlusername***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $username
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'username'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlpassword***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $password
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'password'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqldatabasename***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'periodic_table'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***createanewmysqliobjectwithdefaultdatabase***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $mysqli
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =@new
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysqli
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $hostname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $username
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $password
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /*checkconnection*/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              if(!
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysqli_connect_errno
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ())
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***ifwearesuccessful***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'ConnectedSuccessfully&lt;br/&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***CreatetheSQLstatement***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'INSERTINTOelementsVALUES(?,?,?,?)'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***Initializeastatementobjectformysqli_stmt_prepare()***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $stmt
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysqli_stmt_init
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $mysqli
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***prepareourstatement***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              if(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysqli_stmt_prepare
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $stmt
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ))
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***bindtheparameters***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysqli_stmt_bind_param
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $stmt
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'isss'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $atomicnumber
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $latin
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $english
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $abbr
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***setparametersandexecute***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $atomicnumber
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              1
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $latin
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Hydrogenium'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $english
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Hydrogen'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $abbr
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'H'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysqli_stmt_execute
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $stmt
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***setparametersandexecute***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $atomicnumber
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              2
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $latin
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Helium'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $english
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Helium'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $abbr
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'He'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysqli_stmt_execute
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $stmt
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***setparametersandexecute***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $atomicnumber
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              3
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $latin
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Lithium'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $english
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Lithium'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $abbr
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Li'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysqli_stmt_execute
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $stmt
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***setparametersandexecute***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $atomicnumber
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              4
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $latin
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Beryllium'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $english
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Beryllium'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $abbr
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Be'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysqli_stmt_execute
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $stmt
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***setparametersandexecute***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $atomicnumber
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              5
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $latin
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Borum'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $english
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Boron'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $abbr
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'B'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysqli_stmt_execute
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $stmt
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              else
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***ifweareunabletoconnect***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Unabletoconnect'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              exit();
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              ?&gt;
              <br/>
             </span>
            </span>
           </code>
          </div>
          <p>
           We see above a more modular solution to the issue. We can create code blocks also that are easy to read and easy to manage. Just a note on binding parameters. Lets examine the mysqli_stmt_bind_param() line of code...
          </p>
          <div class="codebox">
           <code>
            <span style="color: #000000">
             <br/>
             mysqli_stmt_bind_param($stmt,'isss',$atomicnumber,$latin,$english,$abbr);
             <br/>
            </span>
           </code>
          </div>
          <p>
           This function binds the parameters to the query and tells the database what the parameters are. Next is the "isss" arguement. This listes the types of data that the parameters are. The
           <span class="codechar">
            i
           </span>
           tells mysql that the parameter is an integer. The
           <span class="codechar">
            s
           </span>
           character tells mysql that the parameter is a string. This arguement may be one of four types.
          </p>
          <ul>
           <li>
            i - integer
           </li>
           <li>
            d - double
           </li>
           <li>
            s - string
           </li>
           <li>
            b - BLOB
           </li>
          </ul>
          <p>
           You must have one of these for each parameter. Prepared statements separate data from logic, thereby aiding us in our quest for secure data. By telling mysql what type of data to expect we can help minimise the risk of SQL injection vulnerabilities in our code. Should any values from external sources be used it is critical that they be sanitized and validated. More on this topic later...
          </p>
          <h4>
           <a class="anchor" name="8.3">
            INSERT multiple records with PDO
           </a>
          </h4>
          <p>
           If you have followed the previous example with mysqli, the step to using PDO is small. The PDO interface allows us to use bound parameters and prepared statements also. The great benifit of PDO is exceptions and use of arrays for queries. For multiple a mulitple INSERT statement would could use an array as a parameter. The PDO interface will also give easy access to the use of transactions. In the following example we will see how to quickly deal with a multiple INSERT. Once again we will use only a small portion of the table to demonstrate for obvious reasons.
          </p>
          <div class="codebox">
           <code>
            <span style="color: #000000">
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              &lt;?php
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlhostname***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $hostname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'localhost'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlusername***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $username
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'username'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlpassword***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $password
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'password'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***databasename***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'periodic_table'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
              try{
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbh
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =new
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              PDO
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "mysql:host=
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $hostname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              ;dbname=
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $username
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $password
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***echoamessagesayingwehaveconnected***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Connectedtodatabase&lt;br/&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***setthePDOerrormodetoexception***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbh
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              setAttribute
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              PDO
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ::
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              ATTR_ERRMODE
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              PDO
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ::
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              ERRMODE_EXCEPTION
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***beginthetransaction***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbh
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              beginTransaction
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ();
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***ourSQLstatememtns***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbh
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              exec
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "INSERTINTOelements(atomicnumber,latin,english,abbr)
              <br/>
              VALUES(1,'Hydrogen','Hydrogen','H')"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbh
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              exec
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "INSERTINTOelements(atomicnumber,latin,english,abbr)
              <br/>
              VALUES(1,'Hydrogenium','Hydrogen','H')"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbh
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              exec
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "INSERTINTOelements(atomicnumber,latin,english,abbr)
              <br/>
              VALUES(2,'Helium','Helium','He')"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbh
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              exec
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "INSERTINTOelements(atomicnumber,latin,english,abbr)
              <br/>
              VALUES(3,'Lithium','Lithium','Li')"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbh
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              exec
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "INSERTINTOelements(atomicnumber,latin,english,abbr)
              <br/>
              VALUES(4,'Beryllium','Beryllium','Be')"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbh
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              exec
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "INSERTINTOelements(atomicnumber,latin,english,abbr)
              <br/>
              VALUES(5,'Borum','Boron','B')"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***committhetransaction***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbh
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              commit
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ();
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***echoamessagetosaythedatabasewascreated***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Dataenteredsuccessfully&lt;br/&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              catch(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              PDOException$e
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              )
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***rollbackthetransactionifwefail***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbh
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              rollback
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ();
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***echothesqlstatementanderrormessage***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;br/&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $e
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              getMessage
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ();
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              ?&gt;
              <br/>
             </span>
            </span>
           </code>
          </div>
          <p>
           Because PDO is a total package it will of course allow us to use prepared statements and bound parameters also. Bound parameters are superior in that they minimize bandwidth the the server as you need send only the parameters each time, and not the whole query. This also reduces parsing time as the preparation on the query is done only once. Lets look at the PDO method of preparation and binding of parameters.
          </p>
          <div class="codebox">
           <code>
            <span style="color: #000000">
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              &lt;?php
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlhostname***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $hostname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'localhost'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlusername***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $username
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'username'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlpassword***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $password
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'password'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***databasename***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'periodic_table'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
              try{
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbh
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =new
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              PDO
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "mysql:host=
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $hostname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              ;dbname=
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $username
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $password
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***echoamessagesayingwehaveconnected***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Connectedtodatabase&lt;br/&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***setthePDOerrormodetoexception***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbh
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              setAttribute
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              PDO
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ::
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              ATTR_ERRMODE
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              PDO
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ::
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              ERRMODE_EXCEPTION
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***preparethesql***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $stmt
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbh
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              prepare
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "INSERTINTOelements(atomicnumber,latin,english,abbr)
              <br/>
              VALUES(:atomicnumber,:latin,:english,:abbr)"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $stmt
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              bindParam
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              ':atomicnumber'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $atomicnumber
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $stmt
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              bindParam
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              ':latin'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $latin
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $stmt
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              bindParam
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              ':english'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">

             </span>

             </span>

             </span>

             </span>

             </span>

              }
              <br/>
              catch(
