          <h3>
           <a class="anchor" name="9">
            SELECT data with MySQL
           </a>
          </h3>
          <p>
           This will be the most used feature of your database. Up to this point we have concentrated on getting connected and putting information into the database and now we will see various methods of getting this information out of the database, and of displaying it correctly on a web page. This is what dynamic web sites are all about. To access our information in the database we need to query (ask) the database with the SELECT command. SELECT will do exactly as the name describes and select what ever we tell it to. Once we SELECT the data from the database we need to be able to display it onto a web page. PHP has many tools for this job and makes life rather simple for us. But lets just get an example happening and more will be clear.
          </p>
          <h4>
           <a class="anchor" name="9.1">
            SELECT with mysql
           </a>
          </h4>
          <p>
           Once again we still need to be able to connect to the database server and select the database we wish to extract information from. So much of the code we have used before remains the same in that respect. It is only when we wish to SELECT and display this information that things are new.
          </p>
          <div class="codebox">
           <code>
            <span style="color: #000000">
             <br/>
             &lt;table&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;AtomicNumber&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Latin&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;English&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Abbreviation&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              &lt;?php
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlhostname***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $hostname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'localhost'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlusername***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $username
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'username'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlpassword***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $password
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'password'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqldatabasename***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'periodic_table'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***connecttothedatabase***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $link
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =@
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysql_connect
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $hostname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $username
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $password
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***checkifthelinkisavalidresource***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              if(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              is_resource
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $link
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ))
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***selectthedatabasewewishtouse***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              if(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysql_select_db
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $link
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              )===
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              TRUE
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              )
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***sqltoSELECTinformation***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "SELECT*FROMelements"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***runthequery***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $result
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysql_query
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***checkiftheresultisavalidresource***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              if(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              is_resource
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $result
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ))
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***checkifwehavemorethanzerorows***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              if(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysql_num_rows
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $result
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              )!==
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              0
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              )
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
              while(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $row
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysql_fetch_array
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $result
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ))
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;tr&gt;
              <br/>
              &lt;td&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $row
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              [
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'atomicnumber'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ].
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;/td&gt;
              <br/>
              &lt;td&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $row
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              [
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'latin'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ].
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;/td&gt;
              <br/>
              &lt;td&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $row
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              [
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'english'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ].
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;/td&gt;
              <br/>
              &lt;td&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $row
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              [
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'abbr'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ].
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;/td&gt;
              <br/>
              &lt;/tr&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              else
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***ifzeroresultsarefound..***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Zeroresultsfound'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              else
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***iftheresourceisnotvalid***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Novalidresourcefound'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***ifweareunabletoselectthedatabaseshowanerror***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              else
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Unabletoselectdatabase'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***closetheconnection***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysql_close
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $link
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              else
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***ifwefailtoconnect***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Unabletoconnect'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              ?&gt;
              <br/>
             </span>
             &lt;/table&gt;
             <br/>
            </span>
           </code>
          </div>
          <p>
           The table that results from this code will look like this, Only first 5 records shown for the sake of sanity.
          </p>
          <table>
           <tr>
            <th>
             Atomic Number
            </th>
            <th>
             Latin
            </th>
            <th>
             English
            </th>
            <th>
             Abbreviation
            </th>
           </tr>
           <tr>
            <td>
             1
            </td>
            <td>
             Hydrogenium
            </td>
            <td>
             Hydrogen
            </td>
            <td>
             H
            </td>
           </tr>
           <tr>
            <td>
             2
            </td>
            <td>
             Helium
            </td>
            <td>
             Helium
            </td>
            <td>
             He
            </td>
           </tr>
           <tr>
            <td>
             3
            </td>
            <td>
             Lithium
            </td>
            <td>
             Lithium
            </td>
            <td>
             Li
            </td>
           </tr>
           <tr>
            <td>
             4
            </td>
            <td>
             Beryllium
            </td>
            <td>
             Beryllium
            </td>
            <td>
             Be
            </td>
           </tr>
           <tr>
            <td>
             5
            </td>
            <td>
             Borum
            </td>
            <td>
             Boron
            </td>
            <td>
             B
            </td>
           </tr>
          </table>
          <p>
           OK, so there is a little to digest here. We see our connection as we have been using it in all our previous examples. The same applies for the selection of the database. If all is well up to that point, ie: no errors, then we see our SQL query.
           <br/>
           <span class="codechar">
            SELECT * FROM elements
           </span>
           <br/>
           The
           <span class="codechar">
            *
           </span>
           character is a wildcard in SQL meaning everything. What we are doing is SELECTing all records from the elements table, five of them in this example. The next line of code runs our query for us and assigns the resulting data to a variable called $result.
          </p>
          <p>
           If the $result variable is a valid resource, we continue with our code. We then use the function mysql_num_rows() to check that we have more than zero amount of rows returned. The is_resource() function does not tell us if we SELECTed zero results. We could have done something like this.
          </p>
          <div class="codebox">
           <code>
            <span style="color: #000000">
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              &lt;?php
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              if(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              is_resource
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $result
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              )&amp;&amp;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysql_num_rows
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $result
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              )!==
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              0
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              )
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              displayresultshere
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              }
              <br/>
              else
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Anerrorhasoccurred'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              ?&gt;
              <br/>
             </span>
            </span>
           </code>
          </div>
          <p>
           The above line would tell us that the result is valid AND we have more than zero lines. So why not have them together and make our code smaller? The answer lays in error checking. We may wish to handle the errors differently. If there is a problem we would not know which problem it is. Is it a problem with the result or is it a problem with the number of rows returned. Sometime verbose code is better for readability sake.
          </p>
          <p>
           From there, assuming we have a valid result and more than zero rows in our result, we use the function mysql_fetch_array() to put all the results into an array that we can iterate over with a while() loop. The while() loop executes the statement within
           <br/>
           $row=mysql_fetch_array($result)
           <br/>
           as long as it is TRUE. This means it will continue looping over the result set and assigning the $row array variable which we can then access and output along with our HTML table structure.
          </p>
          <h4>
           <a class="anchor" name="9.2">
            SELECT with mysqli
           </a>
          </h4>
          <p>
           In our previous INSERT with mysqli we saw how to bind parameters which helped to shorten up our code base. The mysqli extension also supports bound results or "bound output parameters". Binding results helps us as we no longer need to explicitly assign results to a variable. Lets see it in action.
          </p>
          <div class="codebox">
           <code>
            <span style="color: #000000">
             <br/>
             &lt;table&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;th&gt;AtomicNumber&lt;/th&gt;&lt;th&gt;Latin&lt;/th&gt;&lt;th&gt;English&lt;/th&gt;&lt;th&gt;Abbreviation&lt;/th&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              &lt;?php
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlhostname***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $hostname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'localhost'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlusername***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $username
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'username'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlpassword***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $password
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'password'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqldatabasename***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'periodic_table'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***createanewmysqliobjectwithdefaultdatabase***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $mysqli
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =@new
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysqli
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $hostname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $username
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $password
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /*checkconnection*/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              if(!
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysqli_connect_errno
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ())
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***ifwearesuccessful***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'ConnectedSuccessfully&lt;br/&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***ourSELECTquery***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "SELECTatomicnumber,latin,english,abbrFROMelements"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***preparestatement***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              if(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $stmt
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $mysqli
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              prepare
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ))
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***executeourSQLquery***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $stmt
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              execute
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ();
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***bindtheresults***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $stmt
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              bind_result
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $atomicnumber
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $latin
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $english
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $abbr
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***loopovertheresultset***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              while(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $stmt
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              fetch
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ())
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***echoourtablerows***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $atomicnumber
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $latin
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $english
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $abbr
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***closeconnection***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $mysqli
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              close
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ();
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              else
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***ifweareunabletoconnect***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Unabletoconnect'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              exit();
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              ?&gt;
              <br/>
             </span>
             &lt;/table&gt;
             <br/>
            </span>
           </code>
          </div>
          <p>
           The use of bound paramenters and prepared statements are a quantum leap for developers as the increased performance, security and convenience can make scalable, large-scale developments much faster and easier to create.
          </p>
          <h4>
           <a class="anchor" name="9.3">
            SELECT with PDO
           </a>
          </h4>
          <p>
           The PDO extension does not have the richness of features the mysqli extension has but this is more then compensated for by the addition of the SPL class and its ability to create your own extended classes. Here we will use these built in classes to create our table.
          </p>
          <div class="codebox">
           <code>
            <span style="color: #000000">
             <br/>
             &lt;tablestyle="border:solid1pxblack;width:400px;"&gt;
             <br/>
             &lt;tr&gt;&lt;th&gt;AtomicNumber&lt;/th&gt;&lt;th&gt;Latin&lt;/th&gt;&lt;th&gt;English&lt;/th&gt;&lt;th&gt;Abbr&lt;/th&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              &lt;?php
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***extendtheRecursiveIteratorIterator***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              class
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              TableRows
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              extends
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              RecursiveIteratorIterator
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              {
              <br/>
              <br/>
              function
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              __construct
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $it
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ){
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***hereweusetheparentclassanduseLEAVES_ONLYto***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              parent
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ::
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              __construct
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $it
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              self
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ::
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              LEAVES_ONLY
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***usethecurrentmethodtowrapupour&lt;td&gt;s***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              function
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              current
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (){
              <br/>
              return
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;tdstyle="width:150px;border:1pxsolidblack;"&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              parent
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ::
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              current
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ().
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;/td&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***usethebeginChildrenmethodtobeginatablerow***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              function
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              beginChildren
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (){
              <br/>
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;tr&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***usetheendChildrenmethodtocloseatablerow***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              function
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              endChildren
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (){
              <br/>
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;/tr&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "\n"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              <br/>
              }
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              //endclass
              <br/>
              <br/>
              /***mysqlhostname***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $hostname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'localhost'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlusername***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $username
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'username'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlpassword***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $password
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'password'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***databasename***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'periodic_table'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
              try{
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbh
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =new
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              PDO
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "mysql:host=
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $hostname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              ;dbname=
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $username
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $password
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***setthePDOerrormodetoexception***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbh
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              setAttribute
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              PDO
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ::
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              ATTR_ERRMODE
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              PDO
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ::
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              ERRMODE_EXCEPTION
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $stmt
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbh
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              prepare
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'SELECT*FROMelements'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***exceutethequery***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $stmt
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              execute
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ();
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /*bysettingtheFETCHmodewecanset
              <br/>
              *theresultingarraystonumericalorassociative
              <br/>
              */
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $result
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $stmt
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              setFetchMode
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              PDO
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ::
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              FETCH_ASSOC
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***theresultshouldbeaninstanceofPDOStatement***/
              <br/>
              /***IteratorIteratorconvertsitandafterthatyoucandoanyiteratoroperationwithit***/
              <br/>
              /***Theiteratorwillfetchtheresultsforus.***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              foreach(new
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              TableRows
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (new
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              RecursiveArrayIterator
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $stmt
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              fetchAll
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ()))as
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $k
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $v
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              )
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $v
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dsn
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              null
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              catch(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              PDOException$e
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              )
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
              print
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "Error!:"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $e
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              getMessage
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ().
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;br/&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              ?&gt;
             </span>
             <br/>
             &lt;/table&gt;
             <br/>
            </span>
           </code>
          </div>
          <p>
           So, the combination of internal PHP classes and interfaces gives a far superior and standardised method of interacting with MySQL for the purposes of displaying data.
          </p>
          <h4>
           <a class="anchor" name="9.4">
            SELECT Mulitple Conditions
           </a>
          </h4>
          <p>
           We have seen above how to SELECT information FROM a table in MySQL. But what if you wanted to be a little more conditional on what it is you are SELECTing. Eg: you may wish to SELECT only records that have an id of 1. Perhaps only SELECTing elements 21 and 38. To do this we use the two new concepts,
           <span class="codechar">
            WHERE
           </span>
           and
           <span class="codechar">
            AND
           </span>
           . Whichever method you are using to access the database, mysql, mysqli, or PDO, all you need do is change your SQL query as follows to SELECT records which have an atomic number of 21
           <span class="codechar">
            AND
           </span>
           latin name is Scanadium.
          </p>
          <div class="codebox">
           <code>
            <span style="color: #000000">
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              &lt;?php
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***sqltoselectwith2conditions***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "SELECT*FROMelementsWHEREatomicnumber=21ANDlatin='Scanadium'"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              ?&gt;
             </span>
            </span>
           </code>
          </div>
          <p>
           From the above SQL query we recieve only a single result. To take this one step further you could introduce the
           <span class="codechar">
            OR
           </span>
           operator. It works in much the same manner except is conditional on one of the values being true rather than both. This SQL statement shows how.
          </p>
          <div class="codebox">
           <code>
            <span style="color: #000000">
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              &lt;?php
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***sqltoselectwithtwopossibleconditions***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "SELECT*FROMelementsWHEREatomicnumber=88ORlatin='Scanadium'"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              ?&gt;
             </span>
            </span>
           </code>
          </div>
          <p>
           Now we see that the we recieve two results back in our dataset as the SQL has returned any row where either of the possibilities is true. You can, of course, use more than one
           <span class="codechar">
            AND
           </span>
           or
           <span class="codechar">
            OR
           </span>
           in a SQL query to test as many conditions as you wish.
          </p>
          <h3>
           <a class="anchor" name="10">
            Deleting Data
           </a>
          </h3>
          <p>
           Deleting data from a MySQL database is the same as running and command as we saw earlier in this tutorial. If you have read the first few sections of this tutorial then the syntax should look familiar. In this example we will delete the record with the atomic number of 4. In real world situations you would most likely get the number from a $_GET or $_POST variable from a form. This entails vigorous checking of variables for sanity and validity. This concept is covered in the tutorial
           <a href="http://www.phpro.org/tutorials/Securing-PHP-Forms.html">
            Securing PHP Forms
           </a>
           .
          </p>
          <h4>
           <a class="anchor" name="10.1">
            Delete with mysql.
           </a>
          </h4>
          <div class="codebox">
           <code>
            <span style="color: #000000">
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              &lt;?php
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlhostname***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $hostname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'localhost'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlusername***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $username
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'root'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">

              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>

              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $password
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'rootpassword'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***connecttothedatabase***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $link
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =@
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysql_connect
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $hostname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $username
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $password
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***checkifthelinkisavalidresource***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              if(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              is_resource
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $link
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ))
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***ifwearesuccessful***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Connectedsuccessfully&lt;br/&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***sqltocreateadatabase***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'DELETEFROMperiodic_tableWHEREatomicnumber=4'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***runthesqlquery***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              if(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysql_query
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $link
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ))
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'RecordDeleted&lt;br/&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              else
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'UnabletoDeleteRecord:&lt;br/&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;br/&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysql_error
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ();
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***closetheconnection***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysql_close
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $link
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              else
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***ifwefailtoconnect***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Unabletoconnect'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              ?&gt;
              <br/>
             </span>
            </span>
           </code>
          </div>
          <p>
           As you can see, this is exactly the same procedure with other SQL statements that do not return a result set. Lets move on with mysqli.
          </p>
          <h4>
           <a class="anchor" name="10.2">
            Delete with mysqli
           </a>
          </h4>
          <div class="codebox">
           <code>
            <span style="color: #000000">
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              &lt;?php
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>

              <br/>

             </span>

             </span>

             </span>

             </span>

             </span>

             </span>

             </span>

              <br/>

              <br/>

              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">

              <br/>

          <h4>
           <a class="anchor" name="10.3">
            Delete with PDO
           </a>
          </h4>
          <div class="codebox">
           <code>
            <span style="color: #000000">
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              &lt;?php
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlhostname***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $hostname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'localhost'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlusername***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $username
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'root'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlpassword***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $password
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'rootpassword'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
              try{
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbh
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =new
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              PDO
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "mysql:host=
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $hostname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              ;dbname=mysql"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $username
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $password
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***echoamessagesayingwehaveconnected***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Connectedtodatabase&lt;br/&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***setthePDOerrormodetoexception***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbh
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              setAttribute
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              PDO
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ::
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              ATTR_ERRMODE
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              PDO
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ::
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              ERRMODE_EXCEPTION
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***oursqlstatement***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'DELETEFROMperiodic_tableWHEREatomicnumber=4'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***weusePDO::execbecausenoresultsarereturned***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbh
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              exec
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***echoamessagetosayalliswell***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'RecordDeletedsuccessfully&lt;br/&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              catch(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              PDOException$e
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              )
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***echothesqlstatementanderrormessage***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'UnabletoDeleteRecord&lt;br/&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;br/&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $e
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              getMessage
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ();
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              ?&gt;
              <br/>
             </span>
            </span>
           </code>
          </div>
          <h3>
           <a class="anchor" name="11">
            UPDATING Data in MySQL
           </a>
          </h3>
          <p>
           We have seen in previous sections how to SELECT, INSERT and DELECT data from mysql, but there are times when we need to simply UPDATE the existing information. The UPDATE key word is used by MySQL for this purpose.
          </p>
          <h3>
           <a class="anchor" name="11.1">
            UPDATE with MySQL
           </a>
          </h3>
          <p>
           To update an existing record with the MySQL functions is much the same as the INSERT function with the only appreciable difference being the SQL query has changed. For our purposes here, we will be updating a single record and renaming the a field to lowercase, with a capital letter. There are other methods of doing this, but this example shows well the process of UPDATE. Lets see how it fits together.
          </p>
          <div class="codebox">
           <code>
            <span style="color: #000000">
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              &lt;?php
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlhostname***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $hostname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'localhost'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlusername***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $username
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'username'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlpassword***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $password
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'password'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***connecttothedatabase***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $link
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =@
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysql_connect
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $hostname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $username
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $password
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***checkifthelinkisavalidresource***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              if(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              is_resource
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $link
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ))
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***ifwearesuccessful***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Connectedsuccessfully&lt;br/&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***selectthedatabasewewishtouse***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              if(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysql_select_db
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "periodic_table"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $link
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              )===
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              TRUE
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              )
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***sqltoUPDATEanexistingrecord***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "UPDATEelementsSETlatin='Hydrogenium'WHEREatomicnumber=1"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***runthesqlquery***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              if(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysql_query
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $link
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ))
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***getthenumberofrowsUPDATEhasaffected***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $affected_rows
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysql_affected_rows
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $link
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $affected_rows
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'RecordsUPDATEDsuccessfully&lt;br/&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              else
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'UnabletoUPDATEdata:&lt;br/&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;br/&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysql_error
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ();
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***ifweareunabletoselectthedatabaseshowanerror***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              else
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Unabletoselectdatabase'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***closetheconnection***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysql_close
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $link
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              else
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***ifwefailtoconnect***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Unabletoconnect'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
             </span>
