             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'localhost'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlusername***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $username
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'username'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlpassword***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $password
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'password'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***databasename***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'periodic_table'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
              try{
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbh
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =new
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              PDO
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "mysql:host=
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $hostname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              ;dbname=
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $username
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $password
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***echoamessagesayingwehaveconnected***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Connectedtodatabase&lt;br/&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***setthePDOerrormodetoexception***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbh
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              setAttribute
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              PDO
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ::
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              ATTR_ERRMODE
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              PDO
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ::
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              ERRMODE_EXCEPTION
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***beginthetransaction***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbh
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              beginTransaction
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ();
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***CREATEaTEMPORARYTABLEandINSERTarecord***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbh
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              exec
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "CREATETEMPORARYTABLEdate_table(idINT(2),date_fieldTIMESTAMP(14),
              <br/>
              INDEXUSINGBTREE(id))ENGINE=MEMORY"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbh
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              exec
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "INSERTINTOdate_table(id)VALUES(1)"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***committhetransaction***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbh
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              commit
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ();
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***echoamessagetosaythedatabasewascreated***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Dataenteredsuccessfully&lt;br/&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***SQLtofetchthedate***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "SELECT*FROMdate_table"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***preparethequery***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $stmt
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbh
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              prepare
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              if(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $stmt
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              execute
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ())
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
              while(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $row
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $stmt
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              fetch
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ())
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***assignthedatetoavariable***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $my_date
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $row
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              [
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'date_field'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ];
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***theservertimezones***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $mysql_timezone
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =new
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              DateTimeZone
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "Europe/London"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $httpd_timezone
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =new
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              DateTimeZone
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "Australia/Sydney"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $mysql_datetime
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              date_create
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $my_date
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $mysql_timezone
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***setthelocaltimezone***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $httpd_timezone
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =new
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              DateTimeZone
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "Australia/Sydney"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $httpd_datetime
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =new
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              Datetime
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $my_date
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $httpd_timezone
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***displaythelocaltime***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'SydneyTime:'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $httpd_datetime
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              format
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'D,dMYH:i:s'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ).
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;br/&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***showthetimedifference***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $offset
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $httpd_timezone
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              getOffset
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $mysql_datetime
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***modifythetimewiththeoffet***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $httpd_datetime
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              modify
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "-
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $offset
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              seconds"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***showtheLondontime***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'LondonTime:'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $httpd_datetime
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              format
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'D,dMYH:i:s'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ).
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;br/&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              catch(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              PDOException$e
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              )
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***rollbackthetransactionifwefail***/
              <br/>
              <br/>
              /***echothesqlstatementanderrormessage***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;br/&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $e
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              getMessage
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ();
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              catch(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              Exception$e
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              )
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $e
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              getMessage
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ();
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              ?&gt;
              <br/>
             </span>
            </span>
           </code>
          </div>
          <p>
           This sort of time juggling can come in handy in many situations. Even if you choose only to display a single date from your database with the DateTime class, you will be able to do so in an environment that allows you to set you default timezone.
          </p>
          <h3>
           <a class="anchor" name="15">
            Load a CSV File
           </a>
          </h3>
          <p>
           If you are reading this section then you know what a CSV file is. Lets take a look at a quicky that would represent data to go into our periodic table of elements. We will name this file periodic_table.csv and it will look like this.
          </p>
          <div class="codebox">
           <code>
            <span style="color: #000000">
             <br/>
             1,HYDROGENIUM,Hydrogen,H
             <br/>
             2,HELIUM,Helium,He
             <br/>
             3,LITHIUM,Lithium,Li
             <br/>
             4,Beryllium,Beryllium,Be
             <br/>
             5,Borum,Boron,B
             <br/>
            </span>
           </code>
          </div>
          <p>
           We have kept the number of elements to 5 for the sake of brevity and sanity. Using any of the mysql, mysqli, or PDO methods of executing a query will work. All that changes is the SQL statement used to load the file. To load the file into the respective fieds, which are
           <br/>
           atomicnumber, latin, english, abbr
           <br/>
           we use the following SQL statement
          </p>
          <div class="codebox">
           <code>
            <span style="color: #000000">
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              &lt;?php
              <br/>
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "LOADDATAINFILE'/path/to/periodic_table.csv'REPLACEINTOTABLEelements
              <br/>
              FIELDSTERMINATEDBY','LINESTERMINATEDBY'\n'(atomicnumber,latin,english,abbr)"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              ?&gt;
              <br/>
             </span>
            </span>
           </code>
          </div>
          <p>
           Then by running the query you will have successfully loaded the file.
          </p>
          <h3>
           <a class="anchor" name="16">
            Preventing SQL Injection
           </a>
          </h3>
          <p>
           What is SQL injection?
           <br/>
           SQL injection is a type of attack that allows users to execute SQL statements via a web form. This definition is a little concise, as SQL injection relates to a whole class of attacks. You will pick it up quickly as we progress. All problems relating to this type of attack come from a single source, not checking or validating user input. Before we go on, lets see a little example of what an attack using SQL injection looks like.
          </p>
          <div class="codebox">
           <code>
            <span style="color: #000000">
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              &lt;?php
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              &lt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              formmethod
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "post"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              &gt;
              <br/>
              &lt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              inputtype
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "text"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              name
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "searchtext"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              /&gt;&lt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">

             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">

              <br/>
              &lt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              selectname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "fieldname"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              &gt;
              <br/>
              &lt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              optionvalue
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "atomicnumber"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">

             </span>

             <span style="color: #0000BB">

             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              &gt;
              <br/>
              &lt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              optionvalue
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "abbr"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              &gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              Abbreviation
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              &lt;/
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              option
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              &gt;
              <br/>
              &lt;/
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              select
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              &gt;
              <br/>
              &lt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              inputtype
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "submit"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              value
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "Query"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              /&gt;
              <br/>
              &lt;/
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              form
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              &gt;
              <br/>
              &lt;?
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              php
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              if(isset(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $_POST
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              [
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'searchtext'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ],
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $_POST
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              [
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'fieldname'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ])&amp;&amp;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $_POST
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              [
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'searchtext'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ]!=
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              ''
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              )
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlhostname***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $hostname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'localhost'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlusername***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $username
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'username'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlpassword***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $password
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'password'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqldatabasename***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'periodic_table'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***connecttothedatabase***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $link
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =@
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysql_connect
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $hostname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $username
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $password
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***checkifthelinkisavalidresource***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              if(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              is_resource
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $link
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ))
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***selectthedatabasewewishtouse***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              if(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysql_select_db
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $link
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              )===
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              TRUE
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              )
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***sqltoSELECTinformation***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "SELECT*FROMelementsWHERE"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $_POST
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              [
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'fieldname'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ].
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "='"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $_POST
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              [
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'searchtext'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ].
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "'"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***echothesqlquery***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;h3&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;/h3&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***runthequery***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $result
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysql_query
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***checkiftheresultisavalidresource***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              if(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              is_resource
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $result
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ))
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***checkifwehavemorethanzerorows***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              if(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysql_num_rows
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $result
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              )!==
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              0
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              )
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;table&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              while(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $row
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysql_fetch_array
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $result
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ))
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;tr&gt;
              <br/>
              &lt;td&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $row
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              [
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'atomicnumber'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ].
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;/td&gt;
              <br/>
              &lt;td&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $row
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              [
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'latin'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ].
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;/td&gt;
              <br/>
              &lt;td&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $row
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              [
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'english'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ].
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;/td&gt;
              <br/>
              &lt;td&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $row
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              [
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'abbr'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ].
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;/td&gt;
              <br/>
              &lt;/tr&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;/table&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              else
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***ifzeroresultsarefound..***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Zeroresultsfound'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              else
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***iftheresourceisnotvalid***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Novalidresourcefound'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***ifweareunabletoselectthedatabaseshowanerror****/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              else
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Unabletoselectdatabase'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***closetheconnection***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysql_close
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $link
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              else
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***ifwefailtoconnect***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Unabletoconnect'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              else
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'PleaseChooseAnElement'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              ?&gt;
              <br/>
             </span>
            </span>
           </code>
          </div>
          <p>
           The form and PHP script above is not uncommon to many that populate the web. The form will work without issue when given the correct data to work with. Like many PHP scripts, it relies on data supplied from userland, in this case from POST. The values may come from GET or even curl. Lets look at the problem. If we were to enter the number one (1) in the search text box and the dropdown menu set to Atomic Number, we would get a result that looked like this:
          </p>
          <div class="displaybox">
           <h3>
            SELECT * FROM elements WHERE atomicnumber = '1'
           </h3>
           <table>
            <tr>
             <td>
              1
             </td>
             <td>
              Hydrognium
             </td>
             <td>
              Hydrogen
             </td>
             <td>
              H
             </td>
            </tr>
           </table>
          </div>
          <p>
           The results are as expected and the script works quite well, there is plenty of runtime error checking etc, but.. a malicious user may be able to enter, or inject, their own SQL code into the query. Lets change the search text to look like this.
          </p>
          <div class="codebox">
           1' OR latin='Helium
          </div>
          <p>
           Now when we run the query the results look like this:
          </p>
          <div class="displaybox">
           <h3>
            SELECT * FROM elements WHERE atomicnumber = '1' OR latin='Helium'
           </h3>
           <table>
            <tr>
             <td>
              1
             </td>
             <td>
              Hydrognium
             </td>
             <td>
              Hydrogen
             </td>
             <td>
              H
             </td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
             <td>
              2
             </td>
             <td>
              Helium
             </td>
             <td>
              Helium
             </td>
             <td>
              He
             </td>
            </tr>
           </table>
          </div>
          <p>
           We have now successfully exploited the script and injected our own SQL into it. Well, big deal you might say, you can see an extra row. As it stands, this is quite harmless. But suppose our malicious user is a total ass and wants to play dirty. Lets now change the search text to look like this:
          </p>
          <div class="displaybox">
           1' OR 1='1
          </div>
          <p>
           The SQL query will now look like this:
          </p>
          <div class="displaybox">
           SELECT * FROM elements WHERE atomicnumber = '1' OR 1='1'
          </div>
          <p>
           Now when we submit the form, the results show the entire table! 
Most web sites will have a user database, so lets add one to our periodic_table database. Here is a dump of what it may look like.
          </p>
          <div class="codebox">
           CREATE TABLE p_users (
           <br/>
           user_id tinyint(2) NOT NULL auto_increment,
           <br/>
           user_name varchar(50) NOT NULL,
           <br/>
           user_pass varchar(50) NOT NULL,
           <br/>
           PRIMARY KEY  (user_id)
           <br/>
           ) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=3 ;
           <br/>
           <br/>
           INSERT INTO p_users (user_id, user_name, user_pass)
           <br/>
           VALUES (1, 'admin', 'secretpassword'),
           <br/>
           (2, 'lame_user', 'lame_password');
           <br/>
          </div>
          <p>
           With the p_users table in place, our simple SQL inject exploit now takes on tragic proportions. With a little craftiness we can guess that there is an username called admin, or perhaps a regular users username may be known. We can construct a query now to guess what the password may be. In our current p_users database the admin password is secretpassword. Our query could be to test if the first letter is the character 'a'. So in our search text field we put this code:
          </p>
          <div class="codebox">
           ' OR EXISTS(SELECT * FROM p_users WHERE user_name='admin' AND user_pass LIKE 'a%') AND ''='
          </div>
          <p>
           This will produce an output like this
          </p>
          <div class="displaybox">
           <h3>
            SELECT * FROM elements WHERE atomicnumber = '' OR EXISTS(SELECT * FROM p_users WHERE user_name='admin' AND user_pass LIKE 'a%') AND ''=''
           </h3>
           Zero results found
          </div>
          <p>
           This means the password does not begin with an a, lets see what happens if we wish to see if it begins with an 's'. We simple change our search text to this:
          </p>
          <div class="codebox">
           ' OR EXISTS(SELECT * FROM p_users WHERE user_name='admin' AND user_pass LIKE 's%') AND ''='
          </div>
          <p>
           Now we see a minor change to the query and it looks like this:
          </p>
          <div class="displaybox">
           <h3>
            SELECT * FROM elements WHERE atomicnumber = '' OR EXISTS(SELECT * FROM p_users WHERE user_name='admin' AND user_pass LIKE 's%') AND ''=''
           </h3>
          </div>
          <p>
           But below this we see the contents of the table. This tells us the query was successful and the password does indeed begin wthe character 's'. It is now simple task to follow along and get the remaining characters by simply altering the search text again, we can move along the password string.
          </p>
          <div class="codebox">
           ' OR EXISTS(SELECT * FROM p_users WHERE user_name='admin' AND user_pass LIKE '_e%') AND ''='
          </div>
          <p>
           This process can be continued till the password is correctly guessed. Then, we are at the mercy of user. The same method can be used to find a username also. By using wildcards it is possible to see if a username contains the letter 'b'. With a little trial and error, the username and password can quickly fall into the wrong hands.
          </p>
          <div class="codebox">
           ' OR EXISTS(SELECT * FROM p_users WHERE user_name='bill' AND user_pass LIKE '%b%') AND ''='
          </div>
          <p>
           Of course, this type of attack is common in open source environments where it is trivial to access the source code to see what the table names are. But even with closed source, it is still possible to see the table names. Security through obscurity is a myth.
          </p>
          <p>
          </p>
          <div class="codebox">
           /* Does the database contain the letter p? */
           <br/>
           ' OR EXISTS(SELECT 1 FROM dual WHERE database() LIKE '%p%') AND ''='
           <br/>
           /* check if there is a table called foo in database periodic_table */
           <br/>
           ' OR EXISTS(SELECT * FROM INFORMATION_SCHEMA.TABLES WHERE TABLE_SCHEMA='periodic_table' AND TABLE_NAME='foo') AND ''='
           <br/>
           /* check if there is more than one table in the database containing the letter p? */
' OR (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM INFORMATION_SCHEMA.TABLES WHERE TABLE_SCHEMA LIKE '%p%')&gt;1 AND ''='
          </div>
          <p>
           Of course, most haXorZ just want to gain access and will try to brute force their way in. A clever hacker though, may try something like this if promted for a username and password to access the system.
          </p>
          <p>
          </p>
          <div class="codebox">
           ' OR ''='
          </div>
          <p>
           If this is provided for both the username and the password fields, it will always evaluate as true and entry is gained. You lose again. So, how do you protect yourself from this sort of thing? We begin with a simple caveat when accepting variables from users...
          </p>
          <p>
          </p>
          <ol>
           <li>
            NEVER TRUST USER INPUT
           </li>
           <li>
            NEVER TRUST USER INPUT
           </li>
           <li>
            NEVER TRUST USER INPUT
           </li>
           <li>
            NEVER TRUST USER INPUT
           </li>
           <li>
            NEVER TRUST USER INPUT
           </li>
          </ol>
          <p>
           These five simple rules should make it clear that we need to be careful with information we gain from outside sources. With proper filtering of variables, and escaping of data, we can protect ourselves from these types of attacts. Lets run through them.
          </p>
          <h3>
           <a class="anchor" name="16.1">
            Prevent with MySQL
           </a>
          </h3>
          <p>
           MySQL comes with a client function named mysql_real_escape_string that is used for escaping data to prevent SQL injection. The PHP conterpart to this function is mysql_real_escape_string(). When we accept data from external sources, such as a web form or via the query string, it is essential to that the varaible values be checked to be sure we are getting what we are expecting. Checks also need to be made that each variable is safe. Here we show how this may be achieved using the standard MySQL functions.
          </p>
          <div class="codebox">
           <code>
            <span style="color: #000000">
             <br/>
             &lt;formmethod="post"&gt;
             <br/>
             &lt;inputtype="text"name="searchtext"/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;
             <br/>
             &lt;selectname="fieldname"&gt;
             <br/>
             &lt;optionvalue="atomicnumber"&gt;AtomicNumber&lt;/option&gt;
             <br/>
             &lt;optionvalue="latin"&gt;Latin&lt;/option&gt;
             <br/>
             &lt;optionvalue="english"&gt;English&lt;/option&gt;
             <br/>
             &lt;optionvalue="abbr"&gt;Abbreviation&lt;/option&gt;
             <br/>
             &lt;/select&gt;
             <br/>
             &lt;inputtype="submit"value="Query"/&gt;
             <br/>
             &lt;/form&gt;
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              &lt;?php
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              if(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              filter_has_var
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              INPUT_POST
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'searchtext'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              )&amp;&amp;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              filter_has_var
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              INPUT_POST
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'fieldname'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ))
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***checkthevariablesforcontent***/
              <br/>
              <br/>
              /***alistoffilters***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $filters
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =array(
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'searchtext'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =&gt;array(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'filter'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              FILTER_CALLBACK
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'options'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'mysql_real_escape_string'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ),
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'fieldname'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =&gt;array(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'filter'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              FILTER_CALLBACK
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'options'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'mysql_real_escape_string'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              )
              <br/>
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***escapeallPOSTvariables***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $input
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              filter_input_array
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              INPUT_POST
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $filters
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***checkthevaluesarenotempty***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              if(empty(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $input
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              [
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'fieldname'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ])||empty(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $input
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              [
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'searchtext'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ]))
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Invalidsearch'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              else
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlhostname***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $hostname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'localhost'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlusername***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $username
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'username'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlpassword***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $password
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'password'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqldatabasename***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'periodic_table'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***connecttothedatabase***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $link
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =@
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysql_connect
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $hostname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $username
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $password
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***checkifthelinkisavalidresource***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              if(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              is_resource
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $link
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ))
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***selectthedatabasewewishtouse***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              if(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysql_select_db
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $link
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              )===
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              TRUE
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              )
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***sqltoSELECTinformation***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              sprintf
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "SELECT*FROMelementsWHERE%s='%s'"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $input
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              [
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'fieldname'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ],
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $input
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              [
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'searchtext'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ]);
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***echothesqlquery***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;h3&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;/h3&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***runthequery***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $result
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysql_query
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***checkiftheresultisavalidresource***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              if(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              is_resource
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $result
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ))
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***checkifwehavemorethanzerorows***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              if(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysql_num_rows
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $result
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              )!==
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              0
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              )
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;table&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              while(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $row
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysql_fetch_array
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $result
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ))
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;tr&gt;
              <br/>
              &lt;td&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $row
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              [
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'atomicnumber'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ].
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;/td&gt;
              <br/>
              &lt;td&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $row
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              [
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'latin'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ].
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;/td&gt;
              <br/>
              &lt;td&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $row
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              [
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'english'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ].
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;/td&gt;
              <br/>
              &lt;td&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $row
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              [
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'abbr'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ].
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;/td&gt;
              <br/>
              &lt;/tr&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;/table&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              else
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***ifzeroresultsarefound..***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Zeroresultsfound'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              else
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***iftheresourceisnotvalid***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Novalidresourcefound'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***ifweareunabletoselectthedatabaseshowanerror****/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              else
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Unabletoselectdatabase'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***closetheconnection***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysql_close
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $link
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              else
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***ifwefailtoconnect***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Unabletoconnect'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              else
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'PleaseChooseAnElement'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              ?&gt;
              <br/>
             </span>
            </span>
           </code>
          </div>
          <p>
           The code above will accept our input queries as expected, however, now if we try to submit any nastiness in the search text like that below our results will be different than we have previously seen.
          </p>
          <div class="displaybox">
           1' OR latin='Helium
          </div>
          <p>
           By using the above searchtext string we now see that the query and results look like this:
          </p>
          <div class="displaybox">
           <h3>
            SELECT * FROM elements WHERE atomicnumber = '1\' OR latin=\'Helium'
           </h3>
           <table>
            <tr>
             <td>
              1
             </td>
             <td>
              Hydrognium
             </td>
             <td>
              Hydrogen
             </td>
             <td>
              H
             </td>
            </tr>
           </table>
          </div>
          <p>
           As you can see, the search string has been escaped and is no longer a threat to our SQL query. We have used the php filter_input_array with a callback to mysql_real_escape_string to filter the variables from the POST array. This allows the use of the variables safely in our query. Prior to that, we added a check to see if the values were empty. This will prevent a malicious users trying to use other input methods to match two null values, which would evaluate to TRUE.
          </p>
          <h3>
           <a class="anchor" name="16.2">
            Prevent with MySQLi
           </a>
          </h3>
          <h3>
           <a class="anchor" name="16.3">
            Prevent with PDO
           </a>
          </h3>
          <h3>
           <a class="anchor" name="17">
            Last Insert ID
           </a>
          </h3>
          <p>
           The MySQL extensions permit the fetching of the ID of the last INSERT on a table with an AUTO_INCREMENT field. This means when a record is added, the ID can be retrieved immediately.
          </p>
          <p>
           The following code examples assume a database with the fields user_id, user_name, user_email and user_dob. The schema would look like this. Note that the user_id field is an AUTO_INCREMENT field.
          </p>
          <div class="displaybox">
           <pre>
            CREATE TABLE users (
  user_id int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  user_name varchar(25) NOT NULL,
  user_email varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  user_dob datetime NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (user_id)
) ENGINE=MyISAM  DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=2 ;
           </pre>
          </div>
          <h3>
           <a class="anchor" name="17.1">
            Last Insert ID With MySQL
           </a>
          </h3>
          <p>
           To fetch the last insert id with the mysql extension the mysql_insert_id() function is used. This snippet shows how.
          </p>
          <div class="codebox">
           <code>
            <span style="color: #000000">
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              &lt;?php
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlhostname***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $hostname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'localhost'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlusername***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $username
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'username'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlpassword***/
