              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $password
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'password'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***connecttothedatabase***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $link
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =@
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysql_connect
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $hostname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $username
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $password
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***checkifthelinkisavalidresource***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              if(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              is_resource
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $link
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ))
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***ifwearesuccessful***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Connectedsuccessfully&lt;br/&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***selectthedatabasewewishtouse***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              if(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysql_select_db
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "test"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $link
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              )===
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              TRUE
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              )
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***sqltoINSERTanewrecord***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "INSERTINTOusers(user_name,user_email,user_dob)
              <br/>
              VALUES('Kevin','kevin@example.com','1995-08-22')"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***runthesqlquery***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              if(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysql_query
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $link
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ))
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***assignthelastinsertid***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $last_id
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysql_insert_id
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $link
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "Newrecordcreatedsuccessfullywithidof
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $last_id
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              &lt;br/&gt;"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              else
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'UnabletoINSERTdata:&lt;br/&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;br/&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysql_error
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ();
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***ifweareunabletoselectthedatabaseshowanerror***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              else
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Unabletoselectdatabase'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***closetheconnection***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysql_close
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $link
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              else
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***ifwefailtoconnect***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Unabletoconnect'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              ?&gt;
              <br/>
             </span>
            </span>
           </code>
          </div>
          <h3>
           <a class="anchor" name="17.2">
            Last Insert ID With mysqli
           </a>
          </h3>
          <p>
           The mysqli extension provides the mysqli::insert_id() method and the mysqli_insert_id() function. This offers the user two choices with the first used in object oriented coding and the second for procedural code. Both will return the last ID of generated by a table with an AUTO_INCREMENT field when an INSERT or UPDATE is performed, such as in the code that follows.
          </p>
          <h4>
           Object Oriented
          </h4>
          <div class="codebox">
           <code>
            <span style="color: #000000">
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              &lt;?php
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlhostname***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $hostname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'localhost'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlusername***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $username
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'username'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlpassword***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $password
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'password'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqldatabasename***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'test'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***createanewmysqliobjectwithdefaultdatabase***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $mysqli
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =@new
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysqli
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $hostname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $username
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $password
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /*checkconnection*/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              if(!
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysqli_connect_errno
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ())
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***ifwearesuccessful***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'ConnectedSuccessfully&lt;br/&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***sqltoINSERTanewrecord***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "INSERTINTOusers(user_name,user_email,user_dob)
              <br/>
              VALUES('Kevin','kevin@example.com','1995-08-22')"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
              if(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $mysqli
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              query
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              )===
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              TRUE
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              )
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***assignthelastinsertid***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $last_id
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $mysqli
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              insert_id
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "NewrecordcreatedsuccessfullyWithIDof
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $last_id
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              else
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;br/&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $mysqli
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              error
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***closeconnection***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $mysqli
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              close
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ();
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              else
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***ifweareunabletoconnect***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Unabletoconnect'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              exit();
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              ?&gt;
              <br/>
             </span>
            </span>
           </code>
          </div>
          <h4>
           Procedural
          </h4>
          <div class="codebox">
           <code>
            <span style="color: #000000">
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              &lt;?php
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlhostname***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $hostname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'localhost'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlusername***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $username
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'username'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlpassword***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $password
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'password'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqldatabasename***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'test'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***connection***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $link
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =@
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysqli_connect
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $hostname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $username
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $password
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***checkforconnectionerror***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              if(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysqli_connect_errno
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ())
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              printf
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "Connectfailed:%s\n"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysqli_connect_error
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ());
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              else
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***thesqlinser***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "INSERTINTOusers(user_name,user_email,user_dob)
              <br/>
              VALUES('Kevin','kevin@example.com','1995-08-22')"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***runthequery***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              if(!
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysqli_query
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $link
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ))
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Unabletoaddrecord'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              else
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $last_id
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysqli_insert_id
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $link
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "Newrecordcreatedsuccessfullywithidof
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $last_id
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***closeconnection***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              mysqli_close
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $link
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              ?&gt;
              <br/>
             </span>
            </span>
           </code>
          </div>
          <h3>
           <a class="anchor" name="17.3">
            Last Insert ID With PDO
           </a>
          </h3>
          <div class="codebox">
           <code>
            <span style="color: #000000">
             <br/>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              &lt;?php
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlhostname***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $hostname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'localhost'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlusername***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $username
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'username'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***mysqlpassword***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $password
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'password'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***databasename***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'test'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
              try
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***connectionstring***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbh
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =new
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              PDO
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "mysql:host=
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $hostname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              ;dbname=
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbname
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $username
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $password
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***echoamessagesayingwehaveconnected***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              'Connectedtodatabase&lt;br/&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***setthePDOerrormodetoexception***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbh
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              setAttribute
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              PDO
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ::
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              ATTR_ERRMODE
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ,
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              PDO
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ::
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              ERRMODE_EXCEPTION
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***sqltoINSERTanewrecord***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "INSERTINTOusers(user_name,user_email,user_dob)
              <br/>
              VALUES('Kevin','kevin@example.com','1995-08-22')"
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***weusePDO::execbecausenoresultsarereturned***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbh
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              exec
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              (
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              );
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***showthelastinsertid***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $last_id
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              =
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $dbh
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              lastInsertId
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ();
              <br/>
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "NewrecordcreatedsuccessfullyWithIDof
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $last_id
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              "
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ;
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
              catch(
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              PDOException$e
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              )
              <br/>
              {
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #FF8000">
              /***echothesqlstatementanderrormessage***/
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              echo
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $sql
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #DD0000">
              '&lt;br/&gt;'
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              .
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              $e
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              -&gt;
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              getMessage
             </span>
             <span style="color: #007700">
              ();
              <br/>
              }
              <br/>
             </span>
             <span style="color: #0000BB">
              ?&gt;
              <br/>
             </span>
            </span>
           </code>
          </div>
          <p>
          </p>
          <h3>
           <a class="anchor" name="45">
            Useful Tips
           </a>
          </h3>
          <p>
           By now you should have the gist of how to interact with MySQL using PHP. Here are a tips to help you get going when you are confronted with other situations
          </p>
          <div class="codebox">
           <code>
            <span style="color: #000000">
             <br/>
             /***mysqldumpdatabasewithtriggersandstoredprocedures****/
             <br/>
             mysqldumpmy_db--triggers--routines--events--user=someuser-p
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /***mysqldumpdatastoredproceduresonly***/
             <br/>
             mysqldump--routines--skip-triggers--no-create-info--no-data--no-create-db--skip-optmy_db&gt;procs.sql
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /***dumpdataonlyfromadatabase***/
             <br/>
             mysqldump--no-create-info--skip-triggers--extended-insert--lock-tables--quickmy_db&gt;my_db_data_only.sql
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /***showindividualinsertsmormysqldump***/
             <br/>
             Add--skip-extended-inserttomysqldumpoptions
             <br/>
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /***settheinitialmysqlpassword***/
             <br/>
             mysqladmin-urootpassword'my_password'
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /***selectyesterday***/
             <br/>
             SELECT*FROMblahWHERETO_DAYS(datetime_col)=(TO_DAYS(NOW())-1)
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /***resetautoincrement***/
             <br/>
             ALTERTABLEtbl_nameAUTO_INCREMENT=1
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /***startautoincrementfrom100***/
             <br/>
             ALTERTABLEtbl_nameAUTO_INCREMENT=100
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /***selectallrecordsfromtoday***/
             <br/>
             SELECT*FROMtableWHEREDATE_FORMAT(date_column,'%Y-%m-%d')=DATE_FORMAT(NOW(),'%Y-%m-%d')
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /***selectrecordsfromlast30minutes***/
             <br/>
             selectDATE_SUB(NOW(),INTERVAL30MINUTE);
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /***selectrecordsfromlasthour***/
             <br/>
             selectDATE_SUB(NOW(),INTERVAL1HOUR);
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /***selectrecordsfromlastweek***/
             <br/>
             selectDATE_SUB(NOW(),INTERVAL1WEEK);
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /***getthelastdayofnextmonth***/
             <br/>
             SELECTLAST_DAY('2006-03-06'+INTERVAL1MONTH)ASpay_day;
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /***selectonlyrecordsthatappearonce***/
             <br/>
             SELECTfooFROMtableGROUPBYfooHAVING(COUNT(foo)=1)
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /***selectallforeignkeysforatable***/
             <br/>
             SELECTi.TABLE_NAME,i.CONSTRAINT_TYPE,i.CONSTRAINT_NAME,k.REFERENCED_TABLE_NAME,k.REFERENCED_COLUMN_NAME
             <br/>
             FROMinformation_schema.TABLE_CONSTRAINTSi
             <br/>
             LEFTJOINinformation_schema.KEY_COLUMN_USAGEkONi.CONSTRAINT_NAME=k.CONSTRAINT_NAME
             <br/>
             WHEREi.CONSTRAINT_TYPE='FOREIGNKEY'
             <br/>
             ANDi.TABLE_SCHEMA=DATABASE()
             <br/>
             ANDi.TABLE_NAME='my_table';
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /***showallforeignkeysTOatable***/
             <br/>
             select
             <br/>
             TABLE_NAME,COLUMN_NAME,CONSTRAINT_NAME,REFERENCED_TABLE_NAME,REFERENCED_COLUMN_NAME
             <br/>
             fromINFORMATION_SCHEMA.KEY_COLUMN_USAGE
             <br/>
             where
             <br/>
             REFERENCED_TABLE_NAME='my_table';
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /***GetalistoftablesintableAthatareNOTINtableB***/
             <br/>
             SELECTtable_nameFROMINFORMATION_SCHEMA.TABLESWHEREtable_schema='table_a'
             <br/>
             ANDtable_name
             <br/>
             NOTIN(SELECTtable_nameFROMINFORMATION_SCHEMA.TABLESWHEREtable_schema='table_b');
             <br/>
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /***selectonlyrecordsthatappearmorethanonce***/
             <br/>
             SELECTfoo,COUNT(foo)ASNumOccurrencesFROMtableGROUPBYfooHAVING(COUNT(foo)&gt;1)
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /***selectcountofrecordsforeachhour***/
             <br/>
             SELECTHOUR(timestamp_col)AShour,COUNT(*)AScountFROMyour_tableGROUPBYHOUR(timestamp_col)
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /***Selectrecordsfromlastday***/
             <br/>
             SELECT*FROMyour_tableWHEREdate&gt;DATE_SUB(NOW(),INTERVAL1DAY)ORDERBYidDESC;
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /***Selectrecordsfromlastweek***/
             <br/>
             SELECT*FROMyour_tableWHEREdate&gt;DATE_SUB(NOW(),INTERVAL1WEEK)ORDERBYidDESC;
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /***Selectrecordsfromlastmonth***/
             <br/>
             SELECT*FROMyour_tableWHEREdate&gt;DATE_SUB(NOW(),INTERVAL1MONTH)ORDERBYidDESC;
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /***renameatable***
             <br/>
             "RENAMETABLEperiodic_table.elementsTOperiodic_table.nice_elements";
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /***importacsvfile***/
             <br/>
             LOADDATAINFILE'/path/to/xxx.csv'INTOTABLEtablenameFIELDSTERMINATEDBY','LINESTERMINATEDBY"\n"(col1,col2,col3)
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /***selectfromtable1whererecordsnotintable2***/
             <br/>
             SELECTtable1.some_idFROMtable1LEFTOUTERJOINtable2ONtable1.some_id=table2.some_idWHEREtable2.some_idISNULL
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /***naturalsortingforMySQLresults***/
             <br/>
             SELECTsome_numbersFROMyour_tableORDERBYsome_numbers+0ASC
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /***updatetextinfieldnameddescription***/
             <br/>
             UPDATEmy_tablesetdescription=REPLACE(description,'OldText','NewText')
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /***Toggleafieldwithoneorzero***/
             <br/>
             UPDATEtableSETfieldname=1-fieldname
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /***selectintoCSVfile***/
             <br/>
             SELECTorder_id,product_name,qtyFROMorders
             <br/>
             INTOOUTFILE'/tmp/orders.csv'
             <br/>
             FIELDSTERMINATEDBY','
             <br/>
             ENCLOSEDBY'"'
             <br/>
             LINESTERMINATEDBY'\n'
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /***Addacommenttoatable***/
             <br/>
             ALTERTABLEmy_tableCHANGEmy_fieldmy_fieldINT(11)COMMENT'Thisismycomment'
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /***Addanautoincrementprimarykeytoanexistingtable***/
             <br/>
             ALTERTABLEmy_tableADDidINTNOTNULLAUTO_INCREMENTPRIMARYKEY;
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /***addaforeignkeytoanexistingtable***/
             <br/>
             ALTERTABLEmy_tableADDCONSTRAINTfk_my_table_user_idFOREIGNKEY(user_id)REFERENCESuser(id);
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /***removeaforeignkeyfromatable***/
             <br/>
             ALTERTABLEmy_tableDROPCONSTRAINTmy_table_id_ibfk
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /***changeafieldsdatatype***/
             <br/>
             ALTERTABLEmy_tablechangemy_columnmy_columndecimal(10,2)NOTNULLDEFAULT7;
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /***changeafieldname***/
             <br/>
             ALTERTABLEmy_tableold_namenew_name;
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /***Addauniqueconstraintforfieldnamedemail***/
             <br/>
             ALTERTABLEmy_tableADDCONSTRAINTmy_table_email_uniqueUNIQUE(email);
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /***addafulltextsearchtofields***/
             <br/>
             ALTERTABLEmy_tableADDFULLTEXT(field1,field2);
             <br/>
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /***addanindextoatablefield***/
             <br/>
             CREATEINDEXfield_name_idxONtable_name(field_name);
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /***SELECTwithacase***/
             <br/>
             SELECTcasewhenproducts.on_sale='Y'thensales_priceelsepriceendaspriceFROMproductsWHEREid=1234;
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /**SELECTtop20mostoccurringrecordsinatable**/
             <br/>
             SELECTproduct_id,COUNT(product_id)ASnum_salesFROMsome_tableGROUPBYproduct_idORDERBYnum_salesLIMIT20
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /**RESETROOTPASSWORD**/
             <br/>
             Stopmysqld
             <br/>
             nowrestartmysqld--skip-grant-tables
             <br/>
             ****WARNINGWARNINGWILLROBINSON****
             <br/>
             MysqlisnowrunningwithNOprivilegesandanybodymayconnectwithoutapassword.
             <br/>
             UPDATEmysql.userSETPassword=PASSWORD('new_password'WHEREUser='root';
             <br/>
             FLUSHPRIVILEGES;
             <br/>
             Nowrestartmysqld
             <br/>
             <br/>
             /*Swapcolumnvalues*/
             <br/>
             UPDATEmy_tableSETcolumn1=(@temp:=column1),column1=column2,column2=@temp;
             <br/>
            </span>
           </code>
          </div>
